## Diagram 2

```mermaid
flowchart TD
    A[Part Instance Created] --> B{part_number set?}
    B -->|Yes| C[Normalize to canonical_part_number]
    C --> D[Call part_number_search_mangle]
    D --> E[Remove non-alphanumeric, uppercase]
    E --> F[Store canonical_part_number]
    B -->|No| G[Continue]
    F --> H[Add to dirty_field tracking]
    G --> H
    H --> I[Part ready for persistence]
```
